# Random Encounter Engine

This document describes the Confictura random encounter system as it is currently deployed. It replaces the original sample XML notes with the live configuration, the supported XML contract, and a complete inventory of the active encounter tables.

## Overview
- The engine spawns temporary mobiles or items near eligible player characters based on map facet, region type, region name, land type, time of day, probability, and player level.
- The active configuration file is `Data/Scripts/Custom/RandomEncounters/RandomEncounters.xml`. The engine rereads it automatically after writes, so most table edits do not require a server restart.
- The current live tables are dungeon-focused. They cover `DungeonRegion`, `CaveRegion`, and `BardDungeonRegion` on the active facets in the XML. There are no outdoor or town placeholder defaults in the current XML.
- Region names in the XML must match `Data/System/XML/Regions.xml` names exactly when using a named region table. Use `name="default"` for facet/type fallback tables.

## Runtime Behavior
- On initialization, the engine loads the XML, logs the active settings, and starts timers for `DungeonRegion`, `CaveRegion`, `BardDungeonRegion`, `OutDoorRegion`, and `VillageRegion`. The three dungeon-like timers share the first `interval` value.
- `picker="sqrt"` randomly chooses at least one eligible player and otherwise uses the square root of the eligible player count for that timer type. `picker="all"` checks every eligible player for that timer type.
- Players qualify only when their runtime region category matches the ticking timer type. Hidden players are skipped when `skiphidden="true"`. Staff are not considered player encounter candidates.
- Lookup order is specific region with exact land/time, specific region with exact land and `AnyTime`, specific region with `AnyLand` and `AnyTime`, then the same sequence against `name="default"`.
- Encounter probabilities are threshold tiers. The engine draws 0.0-1.0 and uses the lowest probability tier that matches the draw and passes level checks. `p="*"` marks an inclusive encounter that can happen in addition to the normal tier.
- Spawn placement prefers ahead of a running player, otherwise searches inward around the player. Nested mobiles spawn near their parent mobile; nested items go into their parent container or mobile backpack when possible.
- Spawned objects get a `RandomEncountersCreated` XML attachment. The cleanup timer deletes eligible temporary objects after `cleanup`, while respecting combat, tamed creatures, and cleanup grace rules.

## Commands
All commands require `Administrator` access.

| Command | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `[rand init]` | Loads the XML and starts encounter timers. Use with care on a running system; XML writes already trigger hot reload. |
| `[rand stop]` | Stops encounter timers and the cleanup timer. |
| `[rand now <RegionType>]` | Immediately runs one encounter check for a timer type such as `DungeonRegion`, `CaveRegion`, `BardDungeonRegion`, `OutDoorRegion`, or `VillageRegion`. |
| `[rand import]` | Legacy importer for `Data/Import/Premiums`; writes a generated XML template under that import folder, not the active XML file. |

## XML Authoring Reference
- Root `<RandomEncounters>` attributes: `picker`, `language`, `skiphidden`, `delay`, `interval`, `cleanup`, `cleanupGrace`, `debug`, `debugEffect`, and the legacy guard `RTFM`.
- `<Facet name="...">` must use the runtime map/facet name, such as `Lodor` or `Sosaria`.
- `<Region type="..." name="...">` should use active runtime region categories. The current configured categories are `DungeonRegion`, `CaveRegion`, and `BardDungeonRegion`; timer support also exists for `OutDoorRegion` and `VillageRegion`.
- `<Encounter>` attributes: `p`, `distance`, `landType`, `time`, `level`, `scaleUp`, and deprecated `water`. Valid `landType` values are `Water`, `OnRoad`, `OffRoad`, and `AnyLand`. Valid `time` values are `Day`, `Night`, `Twilight`, and `AnyTime`.
- `level` may be a number or `number:LevelType`. Valid level types are `Fighter`, `Ranger`, `Mage`, `Necromancer`, `Thief`, and `Overall`. Current dungeon tables use hybrid gates: common and tough tiers use `Overall`, while dangerous, elite, and rare spike tiers may use `Fighter`, `Ranger`, `Mage`, `Necromancer`, `Thief`, or `Overall` based on the mobile mix.
- `<Mobile>` and `<Item>` attributes: `p`, `pick`, `n`, `effect`, `forceAttack`, and optional `id`. `pick` is a comma-separated list with no spaces. Type lookup is case-insensitive through the script compiler, but current tables use readable script class casing.
- Valid `effect` values are `Smoke`, `Fire`, `Vortex`, `Swirl`, `Glow`, `Explosion`, and `None`. A hue can be appended as `Effect:Hue`, for example `Glow:1153`.
- Nested `<Mobile>` elements spawn near the parent mobile and are useful for escorts or support packs. Nested `<Item>` elements can be placed on a mobile or inside a parent item. A `<Mobile>` inside an `<Item>` is rejected.
- Current authoring convention uses data-derived dungeon tables with probability tiers from rare spike through common patrol. Empty or sparse regions use facet/type fallback tables. The current XML has no placeholder `Mongbat` defaults.

## Example
```xml
<Facet name="Lodor">
  <Region type="DungeonRegion" name="the Lizardman Cave">
    <Encounter p="0.15" distance="6:10" landType="AnyLand" time="AnyTime" level="45:Ranger" scaleUp="false">
      <Mobile p="1.0" pick="GiantSerpent,GiantSpider,HugeLizard,LizardmanArcher,Reptalar,ReptalarChieftain" n="1:2" effect="None" forceAttack="true"/>
    </Encounter>
  </Region>
</Facet>
```

## Current XML Setup
This section is an inventory of the active `RandomEncounters.xml`. Update it whenever the XML tables change.

### Root Settings
| Setting | Current value | Meaning |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `picker` | `sqrt` | Player picker. `sqrt` checks roughly the square root of eligible players per timer tick; `all` checks every eligible player. |
| `language` | `en-US` | Culture used for numeric parsing. |
| `skiphidden` | `true` | Hidden players are skipped when true. |
| `delay` | `120` | Seconds before the first timer tick after initialization. |
| `interval` | `300:600:600` | Colon-separated intervals: dungeon-like, outdoor, village. DungeonRegion, CaveRegion, and BardDungeonRegion all use the first value. |
| `cleanup` | `600` | Seconds before spawned random encounter objects become eligible for cleanup. |
| `cleanupGrace` | `6` | Cleanup grace attempts while players remain near the spawned object. `0` means cleanup is not blocked by nearby players. |
| `debug` | `false` | Verbose encounter logging. |
| `debugEffect` | `false` | Debug visual effects on spawn placement. |

### Current Gate Curve
| Probability tier | Level gate | Level type policy |
| ---: | ---: | --- |
| `0.28` | `1:Overall` | Common patrol; always broad overall access. |
| `0.22` | `25:Overall` | Tougher common table; always broad overall access. |
| `0.15` | `45:<alias>` | Dangerous table; uses a class alias only when the mobile mix is clearly themed. |
| `0.09` | `65:<alias>` | Elite table; uses a class alias only when the mobile mix is clearly themed. |
| `0.05` | `85:<alias>` | Rare spike table; uses a class alias only when the mobile mix is clearly themed. |

| Facet | DungeonRegion | CaveRegion | BardDungeonRegion | Total regions | Encounters |
| --- | ---: | ---: | ---: | ---: | ---: |
| Lodor | 37 | 19 | 10 | 66 | 301 |

| SavagedEmpire | 27 | 7 | 0 | 34 | 147 |
| Atlantis | 2 | 0 | 0 | 2 | 8 |

The `default` row for a facet/type is the fallback table for named regions without a more specific match. The current XML is dungeon-focused and contains no outdoor or town encounter defaults.
